    <td style="width: 54pt; vertical-align: top; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Item 3.02.</td>

    <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="color: rgb(0, 0, 0); font-weight: bold;">Unregistered Sales of Equity Securities.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">On September 29, 2023, Tilray Brands, Inc., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<span style="font-weight: bold;">Tilray</span>&#8221;), entered into a Share Purchase
      Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight: bold;">Agreement</span>&#8221;) with MediPharm Labs Inc. (&#8220;<span style="font-weight: bold;">MediPharm</span>&#8221;), an Ontario corporation, pursuant to which, among other things, Tilray acquired from MediPharm all of
      the issued and outstanding shares of 1000652011 Ontario Inc., an Ontario corporation (the &#8220;<span style="font-weight: bold;">Purchased Shares</span>&#8221;).<span style="font-style: italic;">&#160;</span><span style="background-color: rgb(254, 254, 254);">As
        consideration for the Purchased Shares, Tilray issued </span>1,371,157 <span style="background-color: rgb(254, 254, 254);">shares of its common stock (the &#8220;</span><span style="background-color: rgb(254, 254, 254); font-weight: bold;">MediPharm
        Shares</span><span style="background-color: rgb(254, 254, 254);">&#8221;) to MediPharm. An additional 1,378,843 shares of common stock may be issuable to MediPharm to the extent the VWAP of Tilray&#8217;s common stock for the five trading days ending on
        October 9, 2023 declines below $2.3958.</span></div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The MediPharm Shares were issued in reliance on the exemption provided by Regulation S (&#8220;<span style="font-weight: bold;">Regulation S</span>&#8221;) of the
      Securities Act which permits offers or sales of securities by the Company outside of the United States that are not made to &#8220;U.S. Persons&#8221; or for the account or benefit of a &#8220;U.S. Person&#8221;, as that term is defined in Rule 902 of Regulation S.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><span style="background-color: #FEFEFE; font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">On October 2, 2023, Tilray issued 1,032,616 shares of its
        common stock (the &#8220;</span><span style="background-color: #FEFEFE; font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">HTI Shares</span><span style="background-color: #FEFEFE; font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">&#8221;) to
        HT Investments MA LLC (&#8220;</span><span style="background-color: #FEFEFE; font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-weight: bold;">HTI</span><span style="background-color: #FEFEFE; font-size: 10pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman';">&#8221;)
        pursuant to the terms of a $50.0 million convertible promissory note issued to HTI on July 12, 2022.</span></div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The HTI Shares were issued in reliance on the exemption provided by Section 3(a)(9) of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, as securities exchanged by
      the Company with existing security holders where no commission or other remuneration was paid or given directly or indirectly for soliciting such exchange.</div>

    <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;"><br />
    </div>

    <div style="text-align: justify; color: #000000; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">No underwriter participated in the offer and sale of the Consideration Shares, and no commission or other remuneration was paid or given directly or
      indirectly in connection therewith.</div>
